       +</code></li>

       +                <li class="pre-context-line"><code>      if bin_path = Bundler.which(cmd)
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="pre-context-line"><code>        if !Bundler.settings[:disable_exec_load] &amp;&amp; ruby_shebang?(bin_path)

       +</code></li>

       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="post-context-line"><code>        if Bundler.current_ruby.jruby_18?
       +</code></li>
       +

       +              <ol start="417"
       +                  class="pre-context" id="pre-81"
       +                  onclick="toggle(81);">
       +                
       +                <li class="pre-context-line"><code>      Exec runs a command, providing it access to the gems in the bundle. While using
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="pre-context-line"><code>      bundle exec you can require and call the bundled gems as if they were installed
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="pre-context-line"><code>      into the system wide RubyGems repository.
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="pre-context-line"><code>    D
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="pre-context-line"><code>    map &quot;e&quot; =&gt; &quot;exec&quot;
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="pre-context-line"><code>    def exec(*args)
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="pre-context-line"><code>      require &quot;bundler&#x2F;cli&#x2F;exec&quot;
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +              </ol>
       +              
       +
       +              <ol start="424" class="context" id="81"
       +                  onclick="toggle(81);">
       +                <li class="context-line" id="context-81"><code>      Exec.new(options, args).run</code></li>
       +              </ol>
       +
       +              
       +              <ol start="425" class="post-context"
       +                  id="post-81" onclick="toggle(81);">
       +                
       +                <li class="post-context-line"><code>    end
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="post-context-line"><code>
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="post-context-line"><code>    desc &quot;config NAME [VALUE]&quot;, &quot;Retrieve or set a configuration value&quot;
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="post-context-line"><code>    long_desc &lt;&lt;-D
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="post-context-line"><code>      Retrieves or sets a configuration value. If only one parameter is provided, retrieve the value. If two parameters are provided, replace the
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="post-context-line"><code>      existing value with the newly provided one.
       +</code></li>
       +                
       +                <li class="post-context-line"><code>

       +</code></li>

       +</code></li>

       +</code></li>
